<Review>We ordered focaccia, a pesto pasta, the Marcello pizza, and tiramis√π. The dessert was good, but not amazing. The rest of the food was a religious experience. The quality, flavor, and proportions of the ingredients is outstanding, as is the care with which they're prepared and served.

The menu doesn't actually say what the Marcello is, but to try describing it, it's a somewhat deconstructed pizza, served with mostly cool ingredients that aren't baked with the bread, including mozzarella, prosciutto crudo, arugula, basil, tomatoes, shaved parmesan, and a drizzle of balsamic. It's a unique experience in itself, and should be on the "must try once in your life" list for anyone who finds that description intriguing.</Review>< pics>

<user>116406080367088308135</user><username>Seymour Titt</username>< date>
1618363994987< /date>
<Rate>5< /Rate>< review>
OUR HAPPY PLACE ! If you guys are lucky like us then you have a fav place not far from home where you LOVE to eat. This was our favorite local restaurant soon after it opened in nearby Encinitas 2 years ago and has remained so....though the covid lockdown has made our love affair very difficult at times. Lately things have been moving forward again so we decided to have dinner here on Saturday. I phoned around 1pm and spoke with Sarah who reserved a table for us at 5pm. I really can't believe we go to dinner so early these days because we never eat before 6pm at home but it gets way way busy from 5pm on at this very popular eatery. In fact after we parked our wheels just a few hundred feet from the restaurant and walked towards it we could see heaps of people waiting outside for a table. It's that good ! The very second we arrived at the hostess desk at 5pm lovely hostess Benedetta escorted us to a table on the covered side patio which was already packed out. Soon after we sat down Marco the new manager came by to welcome us. We spotted Vittorio one of our fav servers and very soon he was looking after us. Fresh baked Artisan Bread & Olive Oil plus Balsamic Vinegar to dip arrived at our table. And then 2 tall glasses of Sparkling Rose materialized in front of us. My wife spotted something she favored on the Specials of the Day menu....Gnocchi - White Beef Ragu with Artichokes on Top. Okay we will share that I said plus a Giuseppe Gourmet Pizza - no sauce......Mozzarella, Porcini, Spicy Salami, Calabrese, Baby Arugula and shaved Parmigiano. My wife agreed and that is exactly what we ordered when Vittorio returned. In the meantime I walked out the front ( put on my facial mask ) to take some pics of the folks dining on the sidewalk patio and the people waiting for a table. Within a very short time our dinner order arrived together courtesy of server Ivan ( our good mate ) and everything looked sensational. My wife tried the Gnocchi first while I tucked into a slice of the Giuseppe pizza. Totally mouth watering we both agreed. My wife doesn't drink alcohol so I was scoffing down both glasses of Sparkling Rose...quite nice too ! We had half our dinner boxed to go and ordered some dessert.....Mocha Chocolate Cake which tasted very delicate & very sweet. It was just great to enjoy dinner here again after so long. I said goodbye to the hard working pizza oven guys in the kitchen and lovely Sarah at the hostess desk. WE LOVE IT !< /review>

<gmap_id>0x80dc0d6835e26c31:0xfb386556dcc97898</gmap_id>< Review>
Had a nice dinner to start the night. Between the two of us, we ordered a salad, pasta and pizza to try each thing and also shared a bottle of wine.
We got the octopus carpaccio salad. Thinly slice tentacles that was marinated in lemon juice over a bed of arugula and a few half slices grape tomatoes and olives.
The puttanesca pizza was topped with mozzarella, anchovies, capers and olives. It was salty but beautifully tasty.
For the pasta, I wanted the bucatini pasta with the Amatriciana sauce. The noodle is like a straw, and the tomato sauce was a bit smoky from the bacon. Very good!
We got there early because it is first come first serve. The staff work like a team. Quick friendly service. We got bread with lentils in EVOO and a bottle of water for our table. The staff all wore their uniform t-shirts all with a variety of cheeky slogans of ‚Äúfork‚Äù. The seating is tight, but comfortable. They have a unisex restroom with fun wall art. I‚Äôll definitely be back if I‚Äôm in town again.</Review>

<gmap_id>0x80dc0d6835e26c31:0xfb386556dcc97898< /gmap_id></record></dataset><record>
< Text>
I've dined at the South Park location and had the pizza at The Liberty Station location. Unfortunately,  the Leucadia location was a disappointment to me.

We had reservations at another restaurant down the road and we ended up canceling it because I wanted a good pizza. Boo! My big mistake.

We arrived and the wait time was about 20-25 minutes for a table for 2. Perfect! I thought to myself  I know the other locations is always a long wait.

We were first seated out on the patio. The fans were hitting straight on me and I knew I'd get annoyed so I asked a server if they could aim it elsewhere.
He said no he can't turn it so I said no worries. As I sat there I eventually came to my senses and decided to ask for another table.

The front staff said it would be a wait and I was perfectly fine with waiting again. We were actually sat within 5 minutes.  Our table for two was right behind the high top chairs by the glass window to the kitchen and the pathway for servers delivering the food from the kitchen.  Errr... the walkway was tight so servers walking by would bump into my chair.

Our server was very nice but we barely saw her. While she was cleaning our table i grabbed my wine and held it. She almost knocked it down. Whew...

Food:
* Pizza with pepperoni and mushrooms
* Pasta (forgot what I ordered)
It was okay but it lacked salt. See photo.

The pizza was so bad. I ate a slice and Tupac ate a slice. We didn't event take the left overs home. The pizza was soggy. I was so disappointed.

When we walked out we both said we will never return nor will I recommend this location.</Text>

<Text>MAGNIFICO ! My wife and I had dinner here last night at this newly opened Italian restaurant. From experience knowing that Buona Forchetta locations get busy we arrived around 5 pm. A young lady greeted us at the entrance and showed us to a table in the side courtyard. It was packed out inside and half full on the patio already. A server fetched us a couple of glasses of water as we settled down to peruse the menu.I ordered the house IPA which the effervescent manager Giuseppe hand delivered to our table. A server named Liz brought us a free appetizer of fresh bread & marinated vegetable topping. We had been here 5 minutes and were feeling spoiled rotten. Our main server Luca took our dinner order for a plate of Amatriciana / Bucatini pasta & the Barbara white pizza. Giuseppe the manager came by to say hello again and check on us. In the twinkling of an eye our meals arrived at our table. Friendly server Liz popped by to grate fresh parmigiana on both our meals. And of course I added some chili flakes to my half of the fabulous looking pizza. The pasta tasted so perfect and the sauce just a tad spicy. The pizza was exactly as we used to at Buona Forchetta restaurants....a little crusty around the edge and soft near the center with that beautiful Italian flavor. We ate everything in front of us. We could have fitted in some Gelato for dessert but Giuseppe informed us they didn't have the gelato yet.....we understood as they only opened 5 days ago. We had been chatting all evening with the friendly couple at the next table...Tony & Rachel and really had a sensational evening. Sadly it was time to go and there was a throng of people on the sidewalk waiting to grab our table. We paid the bill and said goodbye to our mate Giuseppe. We will tell our friends and can't wait to come back !<//Text>< UserId.>

< review>
Delicious but expensive. They don't really do the traditional scoop by scoop thing that most creameries do. They have a small, regular, half pint, and pint. Probably the most cost effective way is to split a pint with someone. It's pretty pricey seeing as it starts at $5 for a small and $11 for a pint. The ice cream itself has an extremely creamy texture. It also melts pretty quickly because it isn't frozen for very long while it's getting made. The only real complaint I have about it is that the spoons are really flimsy. Apart from that, they have unique flavors that will appeal to most and they are all done extremely well.< /review>

<Resp>{'time': 1533754390554, 'text': "Thanks for your note and we understand, part of the fun of visiting an ice cream shop is trying different flavors! One thing that‚Äôs unique about us, is how and when we make our ice cream. Unlike other shops that make their ice cream days or weeks in advance, our ice cream is made fresh for you each and every time. Because we are obsessed with making perfect, creamy and fresh ice cream, we can't mix flavors. The reason for this is because each machine is dedicated to a specific flavor and they all take different amounts of time to freeze and churn perfectly. Therefore jeopardizing the quality (i.e. If we churned a scoop of Cookie Dough with Pretzels and Chocolate Chips, it might be melting by the time we churned and scooped Chocolate on top of it). We do offer samples so feel free to try all of our flavors next time your at the shop! My favorite right now is the Watermelon Cream. One thing that‚Äôs unique about us, is how and when we make our ice cream. Unlike other shops that make their ice cream days or weeks in advance, our ice cream is made fresh for you each and every time. Because we are obsessed with making perfect, creamy and fresh ice cream, we can't mix flavors. The reason for this is because each machine is dedicated to a specific flavor and they all take different amounts of time to freeze and churn perfectly. Therefore jeopardizing the quality (i.e. If we churned a scoop of Cookie Dough with Pretzels and Chocolate Chips, it might be melting by the time we churned and scooped Chocolate on top of it). <text>This is my favorite ice cream shop in the bay area. Smitten ice cream is very unique because of the smooth texture, prepared right infront of you using liquid nitrogen.
You may see a huge line at 10pm, 11pm.. but the wait times are low because they have enough machines and ice creams are made in few minutes.
It tastes so good, that once you are used to this ice cream, you don't want to go to those traditional frozen ice cream shops.
Although it is a chain, they seem to use really fresh ingredients instead of cutting corners.

I have tried all the regular flavors Vanilla, chocolate, cookie dough ..
Chocolate ice cream is the best but don't underestimate vanilla.
They have some seasonal flavors too like sweet corn, Blueberry crisp.
Unlike other ice cream shops, It is not possible to get two scoops of different flavors.
They also have trios for $8.00, like Chocolate Ganache trio -- 1 scoop of chocolate ice cream with brownie and sauce.

Initially, they launched at many locations, but later they cleverly scaled back, by keeping only those stores that are in prime locations and generate continuous revenues(like santana row) and closing stores like wholefoods los altos.

This ice cream is pricy but worth it because of the smooth texture, taste and all the fresh ingredients.< /text></record></dataset><record>
